Tati... TX?  Really?  I live in TX now and I can give you some pointers good and bad.  1) Humidity.  LA and WA have NONE compared to TX.  Hopefully you aren't going to Houston.  It's the worst.  Austin is better than most.  If it drops below 90% count your blessings. 2) Storms.  When you hear the sirens go, hit the deck.  There is a tornado in your area.  Have a below ground shelter for you with light and food. 3)  Black Ice.  In the winter you will have black ice to drive on. Most places close in this case during the winter. 4) Temps.  Regular temps are in the high 90s to low 100s from May to the end of Sept.  There is no fall. 5) Real Estate .  Housing is cheap.  Where they get you is property tax.  They can raise it sometimes more than 10% a year. It's not like CA where it is a max of 2%.  There's no limit in TX. 6) Driving.  Get used to HUGE trucks that will run you off the road.  Regular speed limits are between 65 and 75 even close to downtown 7) No state income tax!!  YEY!!! 8) Sales tax is up to 9% in some areas of the state.  Some places will add a city sales tax (Dallas) 9) Austin is a college town (University of...).  Lots of burgers and beer places downtown.  Best weather in the state but still HOT 10)  San Antonio... meh 11)  Dallas... MONEY!!  This is where I am.  Good luck to you here in the Lone Star State!!!  Unfortunately our state is VERY VERY Red.. CA and WA are VERY VERY Blue.  Better get used to that pretty quickly.
I am Texas born.  I love it but you may be in shock when July and August roll around.  Great people, great food and great local culture.  Plus you are going to look great in tight jeans, cowboy boots and a hat.
